          <h2 class="core-section-container__title section-title">
            Hakkımızda
          </h2>

<!---->
      <div class="core-section-container__content break-words">
        

          <p class="break-words text-color-text" data-test-id="about-us__description">
              Aydin Yazilim ve Elektronik Sanayii A.Ş. (AYESAŞ) operates in Aerospace, Defense and Security businesses and has been providing advanced solutions in the business areas of C4I, Avionics, Electronic and Electromechanical systems. Our broad range of capabilities includes products and services from design and development to build-to-print manufacturing solutions like tactical data communication, automated target detection and tracking, radar integration and automation, digital moving maps, multi-function consoles, wiring harnesses, rugged workstations and circuit card assemblies.

We acknowledge that the future of our business depends upon the satisfaction of our customers. Thanks to our highly experienced, talented and innovative workforce, through which we continue to expand our product line and services to meet emerging customer needs.
          </p>

        " dir="ltr" data-test-id="main-feed-activity-card__commentary">Bağımsızlığımızın simgesi 30 Ağustos Zafer Bayramımız kutlu olsun.

        attributed-text-segment-list__content-truncated" dir="ltr" data-test-id="main-feed-activity-card__commentary">Güçlü temaslar kurduğumuz, yeni nesil teknolojilerimizi ziyaretçilerimizle buluşturduğumuz <a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/signup/cold-join?session_redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.linkedin.com%2Ffeed%2Fhashtag%2Fidef25&amp;_l=tr&amp;trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>#IDEF25</a>’in sonuna geldik. 

Savunma sanayiimiz adına oldukça önemli olan bu fuarda olmaktan gurur duyuyoruz.

Geliştirdiğimiz sistemler ve çözümlerle ülkemizin teknoloji altyapısına katkı sunmaya devam edeceğiz.


We’ve reached the end of <a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/signup/cold-join?session_redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.linkedin.com%2Ffeed%2Fhashtag%2Fidef25&amp;_l=tr&amp;trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>#IDEF25</a>, where we established strong connections and showcased our unique technologies to visitors.

We are proud to have taken part in this pivotal event for our defense industry.

With our developed systems and solutions, we will continue to contribute to our nation’s technological infrastructure.

<a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/company/idefinternational?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>IDEF International Defence Industry Fair</a> 
<a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/signup/cold-join?session_redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.linkedin.com%2Ffeed%2Fhashtag%2FayesaAgN&amp;_l=tr&amp;trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>#AYESAŞ</a></p>

        " dir="ltr" data-test-id="main-feed-activity-card__commentary">Savunma Sanayii Başkanımız Sayın Prof. Dr. Haluk GÖRGÜN, <a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/signup/cold-join?session_redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.linkedin.com%2Ffeed%2Fhashtag%2Fidef25&amp;_l=tr&amp;trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>#IDEF25</a> kapsamında standımızı ziyaret ederek kritik sistemlerimize gösterdiği yakın ilgiyle bizleri onurlandırdı.

        attributed-text-segment-list__content-truncated" dir="ltr" data-test-id="main-feed-activity-card__commentary">Yenilikçi yaklaşımımızla geliştirdiğimiz ürün ve çözümlerimizle bir araya geldiğimiz <a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/signup/cold-join?session_redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.linkedin.com%2Ffeed%2Fhashtag%2Fidef25&amp;_l=tr&amp;trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>#IDEF25</a>’te bir günü daha geride bıraktık; ziyaretçilerimizle buluşmaya devam ediyoruz.

        " dir="ltr" data-test-id="main-feed-activity-card__commentary"><a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/signup/cold-join?session_redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.linkedin.com%2Ffeed%2Fhashtag%2Fairbus&amp;_l=tr&amp;trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>#Airbus</a> Uluslararası İşbirliği ve Offsetlerden Sorumlu Kıdemli Direktörü <a class="link" href="https://fr.linkedin.com/in/thierry-ader-07654ba7?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Thierry ADER</a>  <a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/signup/cold-join?session_redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.linkedin.com%2Ffeed%2Fhashtag%2FayesaAgN&amp;_l=tr&amp;trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>#AYESAŞ</a>’ı ziyaret etti. Ziyarette, sivil ve askeri havacılık alanlarında olası iş birlikleri ve ortak hedefler ele alındı.

The <a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/signup/cold-join?session_redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.linkedin.com%2Ffeed%2Fhashtag%2Fairbus&amp;_l=tr&amp;trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>#Airbus</a> Senior Director for International Cooperation and Offsets <a class="link" href="https://fr.linkedin.com/in/thierry-ader-07654ba7?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Thierry ADER</a>  visited <a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/signup/cold-join?session_redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.linkedin.com%2Ffeed%2Fhashtag%2FayesaAgN&amp;_l=tr&amp;trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>#AYESAŞ</a>. During the visit, possible collaborations and common goals in civil and military aviation were discussed.

<a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/signup/cold-join?session_redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.linkedin.com%2Ffeed%2Fhashtag%2Favionics&amp;_l=tr&amp;trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>#avionics</a> <a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/signup/cold-join?session_redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.linkedin.com%2Ffeed%2Fhashtag%2Fwiringharness&amp;_l=tr&amp;trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>#wiringharness</a> <a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/signup/cold-join?session_redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.linkedin.com%2Ffeed%2Fhashtag%2Ftechnology&amp;_l=tr&amp;trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>#technology</a> <a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/signup/cold-join?session_redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.linkedin.com%2Ffeed%2Fhashtag%2Fdefenseindustry&amp;_l=tr&amp;trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>#DefenseIndustry</a> <a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/signup/cold-join?session_redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.linkedin.com%2Ffeed%2Fhashtag%2Faerospace&amp;_l=tr&amp;trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>#Aerospace</a> <a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/signup/cold-join?session_redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.linkedin.com%2Ffeed%2Fhashtag%2Fidef25&amp;_l=tr&amp;trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>#IDEF25</a></p>
